Female Communist Suspects Escorted to Guangdong 146

Ou Meng-jue and Mo Qiong Endure Further Hardship

According to the Guomin News Agency, Ou Meng-jue (i.e., Zhou Ai-xia), a woman from Guangdong who previously joined the Communist Party and worked in Guangzhou, is 27 years old and graduated from Guangdong Kunwei Middle School in the 15th year of the Republic [1926], serving as a professor at Lingdong Middle School. Her husband, Deng Li-wen, is currently doing business in Japan. Ou's friend, Mo Qiong (i.e., Liu Zhen), from Guangxi, is 28 years old and graduated from Guilin Mingde Primary School in the 16th year of the Republic [1927], and is the wife of Su Feng, a teacher at Jinan University. Due to the separation caused by the Shanghai War, she went to work in a shirt factory in Hong Kong's Zhongshan line. Ou and Mo lived together and became friends in Guangdong. Due to suspicion of being communists, they were detained by the Guangzhou government for a month. After investigation and finding no evidence, they were ordered to be deported. Therefore, Ou and Mo boarded the Changxing Company's Asian Queen ship from Hong Kong on the 15th of this month and set off for Shanghai. However, He Luo, a detective from the Guangzhou Public Security Bureau, discovered this and sent special detectives Zheng Bo and Lu Biao to track them to Shanghai and telegraphed the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for assistance. Director Wen immediately dispatched officers to arrest Ou and Mo when the ship arrived at the port and brought them to the bureau. The Third Section interrogated them. According to Ou's confession, she had previously joined the Communist Party and worked in Guangdong, but she has now left. This time, she was ordered to leave the country by the Guangdong authorities. Mo denied being a communist. The Municipal Public Security Bureau, because the Guangzhou Public Security Bureau had sent personnel to escort them, should be allowed to hand them over to the arriving personnel for questioning. It is reported that the two detectives, Zheng and Lu, escorted the two suspects, Ou and Mo, to Guangzhou at 4 AM yesterday (the 23rd).

Dispute Over Revised Road Excavation Rules by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works 147

The road excavation rules for citizens in this city who excavate roads and repair road surfaces due to construction projects were promulgated by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works in the 17th year of the Republic [1928]. Later, various public utility companies, because the fees were too high, submitted a report to the Municipal Government for approval to reduce them. For several years, it was convenient. Recently, Xue Ci-xin, the section chief of the Second Section of the Bureau of Public Works, re-revised the original rules. The repair fee for excavating road surfaces is about doubled compared to the original, almost equal to the road excavation repair fee in the concessions. The procedures for obtaining permits have also become more complicated. In particular, it takes at least 20 days to issue a permit after applying, and the method of applying for permits for emergency engineering changes is considered the most inconvenient by various companies. Moreover, these rules were only promulgated on the 11th and must be implemented on the 16th, leaving no time for all parties involved to consider, which is very obstructive. Therefore, various companies convened a meeting and elected representatives on the 15th to meet with Section Chief Xue to request that the opinions of all parties be accommodated and that the implementation be postponed. Section Chief Xue also approved at that time and instructed the companies to formally submit a report. The companies have done so. Yesterday, the representatives went to negotiate again. Unexpectedly, Section Chief Xue expressed a firm refusal to postpone the implementation, saying that the Bureau of Public Works could forward the companies' statements to the Municipal Government for review within two days, but the Municipal Government's reply would take a month, which would be too long and difficult to postpone, and unilaterally notified the Public Utilities Bureau that it must implement the newly promulgated rules from the 16th of this month, otherwise, permits would not be issued. Therefore, recently, various electrical companies, water companies, and tram companies in the city have been returning applications for road excavation for planting poles, installing pipes, connecting water, and other projects that require the use of roads through the Public Utilities Bureau and refusing to approve them. As a result, various companies cannot start work without a permit, and all users' requests for connecting electricity and water are completely suspended. The companies believe that the central government's promulgation of laws and regulations should still give the people a long period of hesitation so that they have the opportunity to consider and state their opinions. Now, after the city has suffered a terrible war and all industries are declining, Section Chief Xue suddenly revised the new regulations, increasing the burden on the people, taking directly from the companies and indirectly from the users, and suddenly promulgated them within a short period of time, forcing compliance by not issuing permits, and not accepting consultation, which is not the policy that should be taken in the loudly sung reconstruction plan. It is reported that they have united to notify all users of the above situation and requested the Municipal Government to provide relief, and continue to handle matters in accordance with the old regulations until the new regulations are revised to avoid stagnation. I don't know if our municipal party and government bureaus can consider the suffering of the people after the war and immediately make a decision to resolve the dispute.

Jih Sheng Association Obtains Disaster Report from Huoqiu 148

The Chinese Jih Sheng Association recently received a letter from Mai Yi-sheng, Chen Kao-hou, Mai Xiao-zhai, Pan Bing-qing, Tang Feng-lou, and other representatives of the refugees from the Guanyue Temple and the Great King Temple in Huoqiu, leading more than 1,100 refugees, stating that the refugees belong to Huoqiu and all have modest family property, live in peace, and are reunited with their families. Unfortunately, disaster has frequently descended from the sky. The Communist bandits ravaged the front, and the flood continued to ruin the rear. The deprivation of life and the loss of property cannot be counted. The survivors left their homes and fled their hometowns. Bengbu is the gateway to the south of the Li River and a land of happiness. There are more than 10,000 people, but they cannot afford to rent houses and are most distressed. More than 1,000 people live in dilapidated temples. If there is no roof, they are covered in mud and rain. They sleep on the ground, and the dampness seeps into their skin. They also suffer from hunger and starvation, which is overwhelming. Therefore, since the chaos, countless people have died and become ghosts in foreign lands, regretting it in the afterlife. This is the first thing that can be heartbreaking and cried for. Mothers and children, husbands and wives, are forced by hunger and cold and willingly induced to disappear. In total, dozens and hundreds of people are separated, grieving at separation and grieving at death. This is the second thing that can be heartbreaking and cried for. Etiquette is emphasized, and veils are important. However, to endure hunger, they have no time to take care of themselves. Young women beg from door to door, with no dignity, and all sense of shame is lost. This is the third thing that can be heartbreaking and cried for. Spoiled children and weak women are loved unusually. They get sick for no reason, and they look at each other like Qin and Yue [distant relatives]. How can they really bear it, but their strength is weak. Once they are gone forever, they are sad forever. This is the fourth thing that can be heartbreaking and cried for. This time, your association publicly recommended Mr. Wang Du-sheng and Mr. Zhang Ze-pu to come to Bengbu in the name of the White Cross Society to set up two refugee shelters to comfort the refugees. Seeing the difficulties and hardships, temporary donations can't solve the problem. I hope to save people and save the (bear to give birth, out of the water and to the mattress, is to rely on your association, etc. The association's heart for disaster relief is long, and the fundraising has become exhausted. The people of benevolence and virtue in the world should respond to this great disaster and make a wish to bring blessings. This is the time.

Englishman Shoots Himself 149

An Englishman, William, rented room 625 on the sixth floor of the YMCA on Jing'an Temple Road. At around 2 AM yesterday, he returned from outside. About an hour later, he suddenly used his own pistol to shoot himself in the temple and was rushed to Baolong Hospital for treatment but died at the hospital at 11 AM yesterday. The deceased worked for a foreign company on Sijing Road in the Public Concession and was 31 years old and unmarried.

A Married Woman is Suddenly Kidnapped by Her Former Fiancé and Married 150

Chen Mao-zou, a resident of 16 Nansheng Lane, Yunzaobang, Wusong, is a farmer. His son, Gou-lang, is 22 years old this year. Since he was a child, Shen Hong-jiang, a fellow villager, acted as a matchmaker and betrothed Shen Lin-jiang's daughter, Lan-qing (20 years old), to him. At that time, he paid a betrothal gift of 12 yuan and a tea ceremony of 4 yuan, and there was also a red invitation. Later, the man grew up and the woman grew up, and he should have been married, but Mao-lang was financially strapped and unable to complete the marriage for his son. Unexpectedly, Shen Lin-jiang, because the Chen surname was delayed in coming to marry, suddenly remarried his daughter Lan-qing to Zhang Zhang-sheng (24 years old), who opened a cigarette and paper shop on Xiaoshadu Road in Shanghai, last December. Chen Mao-lang found out about this at the time, but Shen Lin-jiang's address was unknown at the time, so he could not go to negotiate. Recently, it was discovered that Zhang Zhang-sheng lived at 106 Xiaoshadu Road. On the 14th of this month, he hired a car, took Gou-lang with him, and secretly went to 106 Xiaoshadu Road. It happened that Zhang was not at home. Mao-lang and Gou-lang then went into the inner room, put Lan-qing in the car, and drove back to Wusong. They married Gou-lang at that time. When Zhang Zhang-sheng returned home, he did not see Lan-qing. After being informed by neighbors, he had been kidnapped and taken away. He searched everywhere for Lan-qing's whereabouts and learned that it was done by Mao-lang and Gou-lang and that they now live in Wusong. He went to Wusong yesterday to negotiate with Chen Mao-lang. The two sides had a big quarrel and filed a complaint with the First Precinct of the Seventh District Public Security Bureau. After Director Yang clarified the situation, he believed that the case involved marriage disputes between a woman and two men, and that the two sides had different statements. He prepared a document and submitted it to the General Bureau for investigation.

We who are left behind can only work hard to complete the unfinished ambitions of the dead, and then we can face the dead.

Ham and Red Pills 157

Wu Yong-sheng's Clever Transportation Exposed

At about 11 AM yesterday, police officers from the Second Division of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team were patrolling the river to the Zhengchang Wharf and saw the Xin Yong'an steamship. They immediately boarded the ship for inspection and saw a passenger carrying a wicker basket in the cabin. The police officers stepped forward to search and saw a ham. They took it out and used an iron pick to pierce the bulrush bag wrapped around the leg, feeling a hard object obstructing it. They removed the bulrush bag and saw a layer of lead skin wrapped around the leg. They were highly suspicious of why the ham was wrapped in lead skin and opened the lead skin, discovering that the ham only had one foot claw exposed, and the lead skin contained a large number of red pills, a total of nine cloth bags, about 9,000 pills. They arrested the person and transferred him to the Nanshi General Team along with the evidence. During the preliminary interrogation by General Team Leader Wang Qin-tang, the person claimed to be Wu Yong-sheng, 33 years old, from Jiangxi. His other words were ambiguous. Because the matter involved smuggling contraband, he was ordered to prepare a document and send it to the bureau for interrogation.

Judge Xiong reviewed the confession and ordered that the case be adjourned for further interrogation. The defendant was released on bail, requiring two neighboring shops to guarantee his appearance when summoned. If no guarantee was provided, he would be detained.

Dr. Wu Lianzhou Discusses Damp-Heat Syndrome 160

Dr. Wu Lianzhou spoke in detail yesterday about the death of Shen Xuejun. Dr. Wu said that Shen Xuejun held an important position as a supervisor in the Export Department of the Jianghai Customs and was in his prime. It is a great pity that he died recently from damp-heat syndrome. Colleagues and friends in the customs all expressed their regret. Even though Dr. Wu had no prior acquaintance with Mr. Shen, he was invited to provide a diagnosis when Mr. Shen was critically ill, but there was nothing he could do, and he felt deep regret. The damp-heat syndrome this summer is different from in the past. In recent days, the weather has been extremely hot, and the epidemic is particularly severe. Patients initially have a slight fever, but after three or four days, the fever increases sharply. A reddish-purple rash appears on the chest, neck, and arms, called "banzhen" (maculopapular rash), which requires careful attention. Families often mistake it for prickly heat in the summer, and Chinese medicine practitioners also believe that it is not yet the time for the rash to appear. Western doctors are even more unaware of its nature and do not pay much attention to it. The rash appears as cloud-like patches with no clear borders, while the papules are bright red and fine dots, and prickly heat is subtly raised and feels prickly to the touch. Experts can easily distinguish between them. Moreover, the eruption of a rash in damp-heat syndrome, including white nodules, is a way for the pathogenic heat to escape, providing an opportunity for the fever to gradually subside. In the early stages, it is best to use acrid and cool methods to release the pathogen, and when the rash fully appears, sweet and bland methods should be used to clear the ying (nutritive) level. If mistreated with drying and heat-inducing substances that injure the fluids, or if attacked with purging methods that cause the pathogen to sink deeper, or if the rash does not fully erupt, or if it subsides too early or does not subside at all, it can lead to death. Patients often lack this kind of common knowledge, which often leads to major mistakes. Doctors should be able to recognize the rash early on to avoid leading people down the wrong path. The disease progresses rapidly, and life may not be guaranteed from morning to night.

Free Talk

Random Thoughts on "Ge'er" 175

— Zhan Lu

Suddenly, a strange and eccentric term sweeps across the tongues of the youth – "Ge'er."

The pronunciation of "Ge" is close to "Wuo," somewhere between "Wang" and "Wuo," a bit heavier than "Wang," a bit lighter than "Wuo," that is the "Ge" in "Ge'er" on the youth's lips.

The origin of "Ge'er" probably lies in Shanghai. With the convenience of railway transport, the youth of schools along the Shanghai-Hangzhou and Beijing-Shanghai lines likely all speak "Ge'er." There is no definitive interpretation of "Ge'er." Some say it is a loanword, a transliteration of the Western "Wile," meaning cunning. However, in the mouths of the students, "Ge'er" does not exclusively mean cunning. Anything special, tactical, or capable can be described with "Ge'er." Now it spreads further and further, no longer limited to young students. In the mouths of all kinds of playboys, it is often "Ge'er" this, "Ge'er" that. Out of ten sentences, at least three or four are dominated by "Ge'er." Then "Ge'er" almost becomes a kind of slang.

In the past, everyone spoke of "Fa Xue" (bloody) this and "Fa Xue" that. Now, everyone speaks of "Ge'er" this and "Ge'er" that. The "Fa Xue" of the past became an ominous harbinger of the Northeast bloody battles and the Shanghai bloody battles. Today's "Ge'er," I fear, is also not a good omen. Since the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, China's stagnation has reached its peak. At this time, still loudly shouting "Ge'er Ge'er" is truly stagnant! Truly bleak!

The proper terms set by the government, such as calling Nanjing the capital and Beijing Beiping, but in the mouths of some, it is still Nanjing and Beijing, never changing. Only this inexplicable "Ge'er," I don't know what magical power it possesses, is able to pass unimpeded, sweeping across the tongues of the youth! Amazing! Amazing!

Record of the Battle of the Datong River by Ma Zhongwu 176

— Wang Quchang

Ma Zhongwu Jinyu and Kun were famous generals of recent times. In the war of 1894-95, he fought in the areas of Tianzhuangtai, Taiping Mountain, and Ganlizhai. With only a thousand soldiers, he resisted tens of thousands of enemy troops, bravely supporting himself, and was ultimately able to preserve his forces. The Battle of the Datong River (in Pyongyang, Korea) was especially notable. When Zhongwu received the order to garrison the Datong, the enemy initially came with light cavalry. He once defeated them in battle. Subsequently, enemy reinforcements swarmed in, exceeding twenty thousand, causing great shock to our army. Yet the Duke still acted calmly as usual. He said to the guerrilla commander, "If you fight with a thousand men, better to die than return to cook for your mother. Only if you are in urgent need of help, report it to me." The Duke asked, "How many deaths are acceptable?" The guerrilla commander said, "Perhaps two hundred." The Duke became angry and said, "Wait until five hundred before you report." The guerrilla commander then had half of his men lie in ambush in the ditch as the left flank and half in the forest as the right flank, supporting each other. They fought for five hours. The enemy artillery arrived and concentrated its fire on the forest. The shells hit the trees, making sounds like mountains cracking. The trees were all broken. The Duke, judging that the attack had subsided, quickly led the entire army to take advantage of the situation. At this time, the soldiers had been accumulating anger for a long time, and their momentum was like wind and rain. Their shouts shook the heavens and the earth. The enemy was caught off guard and suffered a great defeat, with thousands of corpses. The river water turned entirely red. In this battle, the enemy lost their courage and retreated dozens of miles. The Duke was about to pursue the fleeing enemy, but the commanding general, Wei Rugui, had already fled. The road home was cut off by the enemy. The Duke was enraged, clenching his hair and brandishing his sword, personally charging into the enemy formation. He broke through the enemy ranks and escaped the encirclement, bringing his troops home intact. At the same time, Nie Huancheng also dared to fight, depriving the enemy of their spirit, but the commander Song Qing, a cunning official, overshadowed the two men. He was cowardly and jealous of their achievements, and secretly held them back. The Duke sighed and said, "If I could have worked together with Gongting and not been restrained by Zhu San, we would have been able to pacify the enemy." Gongting was the courtesy name of Zhongjie, and Zhu San was the courtesy name of Song Qing. When the peace treaty was concluded, the Duke cried loudly to the sky and refused to eat for several days. The entire army was moved and wept. Later, in the Gengzi Year (1900) Boxer Rebellion, he also repeatedly achieved military exploits. The enemy gave him the posthumous name "Fierce Horse." Today, General Ma of Longjiang is also known for his loyalty and courage. Their brilliance illuminates the past and the present. Is he also rising up, having heard of his family's traditions?

West Lake's Illness 177

— Shancha

West Lake, with its colorfully picturesque scenery, provides material for painters. Its lingering temple bells, gentle breezes, and many sounds and colors provide inspiration for poets. Its pleasant climate and fresh air make the sick healthy. Its clear flowing waves and quiet paths allow passionate girls to forget themselves. Its peaceful spaces and fragrant courtyards allow young couples to spend their honeymoons in ease. Its countless temples and monasteries keep Buddhist grandmothers busy with their yellow cloth bags. Its long dikes and lonely mountain roads allow frustrated politicians and poor young men to wander. And there are many, many more things that allow archaeologists, botanists, geologists, and all kinds of "ists" and "ers" to pick up their microscopes or rack their brains. In short, West Lake is suitable for everyone's needs, and whoever has not visited West Lake will be considered by others to have a great regret. Therefore, people like McCloy (a member of the League of Nations investigation team), who come to China in a hurry and have a major mission, cannot help but steal a moment to visit West Lake, calling it a "pass-by" tour. From this, you can know how much charm West Lake possesses? But, but there is an iron-like law in the universe: "extreme prosperity is followed by decline," and there is "a beautiful woman buried in yellow earth" for both the ancients and the moderns to lament. West Lake cannot be lucky enough to be an exception. Thus, after the brilliant golden age has passed, it has inevitably stepped onto the sad and tragic prelude. And now, and now, she has contracted an incurable chronic disease.

In recent days, in the clear mornings when the little birds sing, the lake and mountains open their tired and sleepy eyes. If you want to get up early and enjoy West Lake's morning makeup, then you will be greatly disappointed. Because whether you run to "Su Causeway in Spring Dawn" or "Echoes in the Quiet Valley", you will surely hear the rough military songs spreading. Even if the mountains are all covered in beautiful sunlight and the lake shines with a sweet and tranquil smile, you cannot help but feel that in the tranquil and serene embrace of West Lake, there is an extremely incongruous tune.

Since the Su and Bai Causeways have changed the small paths with overgrown rocks and weeds into fire-snake-like roads, although the female historians wearing high heels have gained a lot of convenience, the beast-like cars are rampaging on them as if they have gone mad. The solid tires burst out annoying sounds on the ground, followed by rolling up ten thousand feet of yellow dust. When the girls walk by slowly, they will have much more trouble, when they unintentionally get the alert from behind! That loud strange cry will make them carefully avoid stepping aside. When that beast-like thing runs past them like the wind, they can't help but sway their willow waists, hold their small handkerchiefs to their powdered noses, and it is urgent. Good, the smell of gasoline holding the circles in the quiet space takes away the intoxicating fragrance of flowers, and the roaring replaces the crisp chirping of birds in those years. Although this is the so-called application of material civilization, how can our virgin-like West Lake bear it? Therefore, she has listlessly lost weight and faded in color. Even before the lotus leaves have revealed their fragrance, you will hear the lament of autumn insects at the bottom of Geling, and the ringing of the bells that cling to people's heels, it is as if the Diridan-Bell will bury West Lake. This is already enough for West Lake to suffer. What's more, robberies have occurred repeatedly, and the tea-picking girls in Longjing and the Buddhist grandmothers in Huanglong Cave have all suffered robberies. Thus, West Lake has become a dangerous place, and our brothers are guarding it in the shade of the willows and on the dikes. Needless to say, the sword light and the lake light are mixed together. In this way, it will obviously cut off West Lake's weak life.

Twenty-Five Fiancées 178

— Shadow-Dumb

Recently, in the region of Gürglen, a young man was discovered who, over the past five years, had successively engaged twenty-five young women. Thus, he had a total of twenty-five fiancées. However, he has now been sent to prison for the crime of defrauding all his fiancées of their money and clothing. Every time he became engaged to a young woman, he would say that after the marriage, he would repay the money and clothing he owed. When he was sent to prison this time, he said to people, "(This is a very worthwhile thing; I have defrauded so many fiancées.)" On the day the court opened, twenty of the deceived young women came to court. Many of the women said to him that if he could fulfill the marriage promise, they would not prosecute. But he resolutely said, "(No, I am going to prison immediately.)"

A Love Affair of Tears and Laughter 179

— Huang Juemin

A friend came from my hometown to tell me about a strange romance of an anti-Japanese hero during the height of the Shanghai battle. The story is particularly charming, and I write it down below to add to conversation.

Outside the North Gate of my county is the Ning-Shao Guild Hall. The guild hall has an attached side building. Every year during the Qingming Festival, family members bring wine and offerings to mourn the newly deceased. A girl, nicknamed Juan, had just lost her mother and the coffin was temporarily placed in the building. She also went to mourn during the Qingming Festival. Coincidentally, a certain military officer passed by the area and entered to look around. He heard a very sad crying sound. Following the sound, he went to look and was astonished by her beauty, like a goddess. He could not help but stop and listen. After a while, the girl still cried sadly. The military officer could not restrain himself and helped her up, advising her to stop crying. The girl thought it was an insult and was about to scold him, but the military officer continued with extremely gentle words of comfort. The girl saw that he was simple and endearing and unintentionally smiled. She quickly covered her mouth and left. The military officer was lost in thought for a long time, as if he had lost something. Later, he inquired with the people in the building and learned that the girl's family was in decline and lacked the funds to bury her mother. Therefore, she had no choice but to temporarily place the coffin in the building. He urgently returned to the military headquarters and ordered a guard to send five hundred gold coins to the girl's family, saying that he knew the girl's family was suffering from a lack of funds to bury her mother. These five hundred gold coins were a small token of his sincerity. The girl had an older brother who was initially very shocked. He then learned the story from the girl and expressed extreme dissatisfaction. He believed that the gift of gold must have ulterior motives and wanted to refuse it. However, he was also afraid of the other party's armed status. As he was hesitating, the girl insisted that it could not be refused. In the end, he had no choice but to accept it. Before long, the matchmaker of the military officer arrived, expressing the officer's admiration for the girl and his desire to marry her to manage his household. The girl's brother was originally a merchant and was at a loss, not knowing how to respond. He urgently discussed it with the girl and blamed her for insisting on accepting the gift of gold, which led to today's changes. At first, the girl blushed and lowered her head without saying a word. Then, she resolutely expressed her willingness to follow the military officer and even threatened to die for it. The girl's brother, seeing that her determination could not be changed, had no choice but to agree. Thus, this charming and amusing love affair spread throughout the county until today.

Worth Introducing National Goods Factories (8) 180

— He Gongxing

(Thirteen) Plaster Model Factory

Plaster models are decorations for desks or walls. Those who draw use them for sketching or as specimen models. The sales volume is very large. Rome, Greece, France, and other countries produce exquisite goods, lifelike. Japanese goods are also imported, but the work is rough and far inferior to Western goods. However, because they are cheap, they can still be sold in our country. In the tenth year of the Republic of China, Qi Guanshan of Shanghai returned from Japan. Using what he had learned in Japan, he established the Plaster Art and Craft Factory in Daji Road, West Gate of Shanghai. He reproduced various character portraits and the business was quite good. Although it was a small-capital craft, it was also appreciated by contemporary artists.

Following the Art Factory, there were two others, the Mei-Yi and Zhonghua, both founded by graduates of art schools. To date, there are three in the entire city of Shanghai. Mei-Yi is on Caishi Road, and Zhonghua is on Avenue Albert.

Gypsum is produced in Sichuan, Hubei, and other provinces in our country. The market price is more than four yuan per dan. Shanghai Labor Seng Road's Rui Tai Stone Powder Factory and Xiaodu Road's Shunchang Stone Powder Factory specialize in mechanically producing various white stone powders, including gypsum powder, which is also sold. The value is about nine yuan per dan. Although stone powder is more than twice as expensive as gypsum, using stone powder can save a grinding process.

Manufacturing plaster models is entirely a manual industry, but it uses molds. The size of the capital depends on the number of molds in the factory. Even as little as one or two hundred yuan can be used to start a business.

Each character model must be a combination of multiple molds; otherwise, after the plaster powder is in the mold, it will not be easy to remove. However, simple ones may only have one mold. Character portraits with curves are often added separately; otherwise, they cannot be complete.

For example, to reproduce portraits of great men, first sculpt the shape with clay, then make a mold, and then turn the plaster statue. As long as the mold is not broken, plaster statues can be made every day.

The manufacturing method is to mix gypsum powder with suitable water and put it into the mold. Wait until it is slightly dry, take it out, and decorate it. As for the sculpting craft, it is impossible without specialized training.

(Fourteen) Elastic Bands

Elastic bands have always been Japanese goods. In the ninth year of the Republic of China, Hong Yu Band Factory in Tiantong An Road, Zhabei, was the first Chinese manufacturer of elastic bands. However, it closed down soon after. Currently, there are eight manufacturers of elastic bands in Shanghai: De Long, on Ma Huo Road; Xin Shi, on South Chengdu Road; Hui Chang, on Yangshupu Road; Changcheng, on Zhoushan Road; Mei De, on Nanyang Bridge; Lin Yin, on Lin Yin Road; Hong Long, on Hai Chao Temple Road; and Jingmei, on Hui Ning Road. De Long is the largest, and its output is also greater.

The biggest use of elastic bands is for making sock garters and suspenders, divided into cotton and silk. Most of the ones commonly used on the market are woven with 80-count mercerized thread, rayon, and rubber bands. The narrowest are only three cents wide, and the widest are one inch and four cents wide. Narrow bands are mostly woven with iron hand looms, while wide bands are mostly woven with wooden flat looms. There are many colors, and the width varies, so the price is very uneven. Each board has twelve yards. In addition to the products of the eight Shanghai factories being sold well in various ports, the elastic bands produced by Suzhou Meilun Factory are also sold in Shanghai because they are cheap and good, and especially welcomed by Shanghai people. Unfortunately, the raw materials are all foreign goods, and rubber bands must be Japanese goods.

Records of Knocking the Bell at the Old Temple (53) 181

— Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu

Fifty-nine

I said, "(The reason why the old temple was able to mobilize the entire village as soldiers is mostly because Battalion Commander Jiang was willing to go to the countryside to fulfill his obligations. If this were promoted throughout the country, how many retired military officers would be willing to serve as instructors?" Mr. Zhu said, "(Now the country has more than two million troops. If the troops in various places take on this responsibility, then the instructors are readily available, the trainees are readily available, and the firearms are readily available. It won't take long to build the Republic of China into a steel-cast country that no one can destroy. The biggest difficulty now is that everyone does not understand their own responsibilities. As long as the people recognize that protecting the country and villages is their own responsibility, and the troops in various places also recognize that training the people for self-defense is their duty, everything else will be easy.)"

Sixty

I asked again, "(Now that the country has reached a critical juncture of life and death, what other training should the Chinese nation receive besides military training to be able to revive, turn danger into safety?" Mr. Zhu said, ")Education is racing against the national crisis. In my opinion, the Chinese nation should receive six major trainings together to overcome the difficulties. These six major trainings are:

First, universal military training, so that everyone becomes a healthy son of the country. Second, universal production training, so that everyone becomes a wealth-creating worker. Third, universal scientific training, so that everyone can use their minds in their labor. Fourth, universal literacy training, so that everyone can obtain symbols for conveying thoughts. This Week's New York Stock Market is Thriving 187

(U.S. East Silver Company Weekend Report)

This week's New York stock market found a good sign unseen since the beginning of the wood year. Recently, there have been many good developments in international politics, and U.S. general industry and commerce have also found solid signs of progress. Therefore, since Wednesday, stock market prices have continued to rise. Public bonds have begun to rebound since the beginning of this month, and have become increasingly strong recently. In terms of transactions, general brokers still took a wait-and-see attitude at first. By Friday, the transaction volume reached 1.4 million shares. At this time, the market began to return to a high level of activity. This week, the Dow Jones three indexes have made solid progress, among which the automotive, railway, food, shipping, and entertainment stocks are the strongest. On Friday, there was a lot of good news in the economic world. The hope of the U.S. Steel Corporation (i.e. US Steel) restoring dividends, and the recent production rate of the national steel industry are also continuing to progress. Last week's automobile production increased to 5,219 vehicles. The profits earned by the railway industry in the first half of this year are still satisfactory. The unemployment relief plan has been approved by President Hoover, which can remove general anxieties. The current stock market situation is indeed very good. Although according to market experience, a reaction may occur next week, the stock market is likely to take the opportunity to sell after a sharp rise. This will not hinder the overall trend. If commerce can improve day by day in the future, people's hearts will become stronger and stronger, and the stock market will recover from stripping, this is the time. Continued Rise in Yarn Prices 188

Cotton Yarn Market Conditions: Prices continue to rise, mainly due to successive purchases from various Guangdong and South China merchants. Existing Shanghai yarn has been almost entirely bought up, leading to talks of shortages. However, some manufacturers still have stock, although the most popular yarns are in short supply. In the past two days, Guangdong merchants have primarily purchased yarn with delivery dates of eight, nine, and thirteen months, causing continued market tension. It is estimated that Guangdong and Yunnan merchants have bought approximately 30,000 to 50,000 units of spot and futures contracts in the past few days, mostly futures contracts that have not yet been shipped. Inquiries reveal that buyers maintain strong expectations for higher prices, due to recent extremely hot weather reducing production in various factories, increasing the number of buyers. However, some have considered short selling, and the bullish side has seen some profit-taking.

People's Standard (Ren Biao) Breaks Through 50 Taels: At the opening of the People's Standard market, it was rumored that demand was strong the previous day, and market sentiment was particularly tight. Individual investors covered their positions, with prices rising by 8 to 9 candareens across all months. In the second and third trading sessions, new short positions were opened, slightly flattening the market. Ultimately, the current month rose by 1 tael and 3 candareens, and distant months rose by 4 to 5 candareens. Total trading volume was 42,000 bales. US Cotton Cooperative Sold 100,000 Bales Last Week 191

Dry Weather Does Not Hinder New Cotton Crop

New York, July 22 Telegram reports on the past week's cotton market: The cotton market fluctuated within limited ranges this week. The impact of the current weather on the final cotton harvest is still uncertain, which has restricted trading. Limited profit-taking and sales were absorbed by short covering and industry buying. Except for occasional showers, the weather remains dry, and maximum temperatures in many areas have risen to or above 100 degrees Fahrenheit. This is considered beneficial in controlling boll weevil infestations. However, the sudden heat following rainfall has caused boll shedding and deterioration of cotton quality in some areas. There are expectations that if the heatwave continues for another week, production conditions will rapidly decline. Small batches of October contracts have been sold frequently, and it is estimated that cooperative brokers sold a total of 100,000 bales in the past ten days, which has drawn criticism. It is expected that futures trading will become more active when the new cotton crop begins to be listed. Weekend statistics are attached below (in thousands of bales):

Less than Ten Ships Arrived at New Zhabei Yesterday; Limited Arrivals of Northern Japonica Rice, Spot Transactions Near 1,000 Shi; High-quality prices stabilized, ordinary grades rose by 2 to 3 chi; Kunshan and Jiangyin rice also followed with similar gains. Foreign Rice Recovers by 5 Fen 194

Foreign rice sales were relatively active yesterday. Ningbo merchants continued to ship. Local sales were also strong, and prices saw a slight rebound of several fen. If there are more significant sales today and tomorrow, the market may become firmer. The general market opened with 6,500 bags of small-grain rice, of which 1,000 bags of old small-grain rice were shipped by Ningbo merchants, and the rest were distributed to local and inland villages. New small-grain rice was priced between 9.10 and 8.85 yuan, old small-grain rice between 8.80 and 8.75 yuan. Additionally, 1,000 bags of red small-grain rice were shipped to Ningbo merchants at a price of 8 yuan. Old small-grain and red rice were both 5 fen higher than other grades. In addition to small-grain rice, 100 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled Yuan rice were sold locally at a price of 13.97 yuan.

Flour Market Showing Strength 195

Foreign Wheat Prices Reported Higher... Tianjin Sales Active

After the opening of the flour market yesterday morning, all months saw slightly increased market sentiment due to foreign wheat prices being reported approximately 4 jiao higher. Therefore, opening prices were stable. Later, outside bullish investors, noting that Tianjin was purchasing large quantities of spot flour, believed that sales would become active in the future and continued to buy, causing prices to rise rapidly. Manufacturers, except for Fufeng, showed little activity. Therefore, the market was exceptionally strong. However, it should be noted that if local flour prices become too high, imported flour will inevitably follow suit and increase orders. As a result, the current month rose by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day, August rose by 2.5 fen, September rose by 2.25 fen, and October to December each rose by 1.75 fen.

Wheat Futures Market Booming 196

After the opening of the wheat futures market yesterday morning, all months suddenly showed booming market conditions. At the beginning of trading, market sentiment was firm due to foreign wheat prices being reported 4 jiao higher. Later, due to the strong flour market, outside bullish investors raised prices accordingly, as if both the flour and wheat markets were similarly speculative. At present, commodity prices are too low, which is greatly impacting farmers' livelihoods. This situation is not necessarily bad. However, the wheat owned by farmers has already been sold, and the beneficiaries are none other than merchants. As a result, the current month rose by 5 fen compared to the previous day, August rose by 6 fen, September and October rose by 5 fen, and November rose by 4 fen. Spot wheat market conditions: due to rising standards, high-quality goods are in demand. Chuzhou wheat opened at 3.2 taels, Suqian wheat at 3.11 taels, Danyang wheat at 2.99 taels, Taicang wheat at 2.856 taels, Jiading wheat at 2.83 taels, and Lujiabang wheat at 2.83 taels, with over 1,500 bags opened.

Discourse

Mussolini's Words 203

— Fo

Italian Prime Minister Mussolini recently explained the meaning of Fascism, with several statements including:

From the perspective of Fascism, life is a struggle. Every individual must first restrain themselves to forge themselves into a valuable tool capable of serving themselves, serving the country, and serving the people. Originally, whatever a person does, they must first set an example for themselves to be effective. If one cannot restrain oneself first, and then wants to restrain others, this is simply impossible. Therefore, the ancients had a saying, "If you want to establish yourself, establish others; if you want to achieve yourself, achieve others." If you want to establish and achieve yourself but do not want to establish and achieve others, this is focusing solely on self-cultivation and completely not understanding the principle of empathy. Therefore, if you want others to be established and achieved, you must first establish and achieve yourself. If you want others to restrain themselves, you must first restrain yourself so that you are not subject to criticism and can be effective.

Since Italian Prime Minister Mussolini organized the Blackshirt Party, it has achieved considerable success. As a result, those inclined towards militarism have become eager to try. The organization of Fascism by Japanese warlords is an example of this. However, the political ideology of a country originally arises in response to the political environment. Therefore, a political situation of one era gives rise to the political ideology of that era. Since the European War, political thought has undergone a sudden change. One type is active Blackshirtism, and the other is passive Communism. These two ideologies were born in response to this trend and have achieved considerable success. However, which ideology is suitable for our country to adapt to the trend depends on the national conditions and the national character, and there is no need to discuss it further.

However, Mussolini's statement that one must first restrain oneself in order to serve the country and serve the people is truly a profound and famous saying. If one can put these words into practice, regardless of the ideology, whether in power or in opposition, it will naturally be effective. For example, Indian Gandhi advocates non-resistance and sets an example everywhere, restraining himself. How is his ability to influence others? What is the effect of what he does? Otherwise, even if one shouts about what ideology and what policies every day, it will only be a waste of effort.

Can the Environment be Reformed? A Discussion at the Society for Social Reform 204

— Proposal by Huang Juemin

Can the environment be reformed? This is the proposal I have submitted to the Society for Social Reform. Below is my personal discussion of this issue.

Speaking of reforming the environment, the first step, I feel, is to first clarify the true meaning of the environment. To understand the true meaning of the environment, it is best to cite Dewey's theory.

Dewey said: "(Environment is a specialized term in biology and occupies a very important position in the concept of evolution. All organic bodies, on the one hand, must rely on surrounding objects to maintain their lives, and on the other hand, these objects surrounding them can affect their activities)."

Based on this passage, we can derive two key points:

(1) All circumstances that promote biological activity are the environment.

(2) All circumstances that hinder biological activity are also the environment.

However, the environment we usually refer to mostly refers to the latter, and the scope of discussion in this article is also limited to the latter.

I dare say that, except for the "son of heaven", most people are dominated by the environment and oppressed by the environment. Is this domination, this oppression, fundamentally impossible for us to escape? I also dare say that, except for "madmen", everyone can reform their environment, because only madmen will not move their feet but will create thousands of difficulties in their minds.

So, what are the methods for reforming the environment? Based on my experience in fighting the environment in recent years, I believe there are four effective methods:

(1) Strong will! This point is clear to everyone, but it is the most difficult for everyone to achieve. In fact, I feel that since people must ultimately live and be active on the earth, they should not think that they have failed and fled at the first sign of difficulty and obstruction in life. They must possess a persevering will and fight the environment to the end. The ability to reform the environment relies on determination, and the ability to reform to the end relies on perseverance. I hope everyone will not forget this sentence.

(2) Extreme Patience: To solve problems, you must go through considerable procedures and time. The more difficult the problem, the more troublesome the solution procedures are and the longer the time it takes. This is an unbreakable fact that cannot be tricked. Therefore, when we are solving a problem, we must have extreme patience and tolerate the necessary passage of trouble and time.

(3) Beautiful Habits! In the process of striving to reform the environment, you must develop extremely beautiful habits to continue to struggle constantly. This habit is that when difficult problems come, we only allow them to arouse our consideration, and we do not allow them to arouse our worries. Only in this way, although the external pressure is severe, and our body and mind are inevitably exhausted due to our efforts to cope with difficulties, we can maintain mental composure and inner peace, and not be internally injured as a result, and can nurture our strength to continue to fight the environment. The final victory will inevitably belong to us.

(4) Appropriate Ambition! Any career that is within my ability and that I desire is an appropriate ambition. I believe that our contribution to society is not to become so-called great people. As long as each person makes the greatest possible effort to contribute to the best of their ability, that is the greatest contribution to society. If it can be weighed, I believe that such a contribution is by no means smaller than the contribution of great people. Perhaps in some places, the contribution of great people is not as great as such a contribution. Our worst mentality is to specialize in admiring the accomplished careers of others, or to be driven by vanity, resulting in suppressing our own strengths and failing to achieve any success. Therefore, we fall into a painful environment and cannot extricate ourselves. Therefore, if you want to reform the environment, you must follow a path that is within your ability to be invincible.

People oppressed by the environment! What do you think of these contributions? If it is not correct, please advise. If it is correct, please do it quickly. A bright realm is in front of us!

Regarding the Proposal to Publish a Special Issue and That Non-Members Should Also be Allowed to Participate in Discussions to Achieve Great Results 205

To the Editor: I recently saw the short notice and several articles of the Society for Social Reform, and I am very impressed! In accordance with Article 2 of the charter, I venture to offer two suggestions, not knowing if they are appropriate. I hope they will be discussed and decided upon! Sincerely, Shanghai Newspaper Local Supplement, Society for Social Reform.

Sincerely, Xiao Kangshi, July 22

1. For all writings within the scope of the Society for Social Reform discussion, I believe that a special issue should be published, once or twice every weekday, to clarify the boundaries and awaken the minds.

2. All non-members should also be allowed to participate in discussions, and once they are recorded, they should be advanced to membership and strive to implement them to achieve great results, so as not to lose the will of the Society for Social Reform.

(Note: (The matter of issuing a special issue in the previous article needs to be discussed with the museum authorities before it can be handled. The original intention of the latter article that non-members can also participate in discussions was originally like this, so the gentlemen who contribute to this journal include both those who have contributed and those who have not contributed. - Editor's Note)

Literature and Art

Feelings on the Recent Hot Weather 206

— Songfu

Get up early in the morning to enjoy the fresh coolness,

Stand quietly by the pond, feeling free and fragrant.

Waiting until noon when the fiery parasol is unfurled,

A good way to dream of yellow millet.

The Slight Heat is no different from the Great Heat,

Drenched in sweat, copying the Yellow Court Scripture.

The god of heaven wickedly releases the fiery power,

Raising the temperature to ninety degrees.

Reflections on the Battlefield 207

Bloodstains and corpses everywhere,

Gazing at the Shanghai shore, full of sorrow.

Every time the wind and rain whistle at night,

Ghostly wails and divine roars never cease.

At the Sichuan Bridge, life and death are judged,

The situation after the catastrophe is naturally sad.

Looking south, the city streets are still bustling,

Looking north, the roads are truly desolate.

Golden pavilions and towers turned to ashes,

When will the lives of commoners and bones be buried?

The most prosperous and flourishing place in the past,

Now transformed into a pile of rubble.

Science

The Manufacturing of Spirits 208

— Lüshuang

Answering Mr. Pingzhang

The method of manufacturing spirits cannot be fully explained in just one or two pieces of paper. Since you have asked, I will simply describe what I know to the best of my ability.

(1) The Method of Manufacturing Methanol: Place wood blocks in an iron still for dry distillation. The still has only one outlet, so that the evaporated substances can be released while outside air cannot enter. After all the volatile substances have been evaporated, what remains is charcoal, which can be used as fuel. The evaporated substances are passed through a condenser. A portion of it becomes liquid, while another portion remains as gas, containing light gas, carbon monoxide, etc., which can be passed into a gas storage tank and used as fuel. The condensed liquid contains tar, one percent methanol, five to eight percent acetic acid, and a small amount of acetone. Tar is insoluble in water, while the rest are soluble in water, so the tar can be separated. However, this aqueous solution still contains a small amount of tar, which can be removed by low-temperature distillation, as tar has a high boiling point and will not evaporate. This evaporated substance is called Pyroligneous acid, and it still contains methanol, acetic acid, and a small amount of acetone. Then, use lime to neutralize the acetic acid to form non-volatile calcium acetate: 2CH3COOH (acetic acid) + CaO (lime) → (CH3COO)2Ca + H2O. Distill again to obtain a mixed liquid of methanol and ketone. Ketone evaporates more easily than methanol, so fractional distillation can be used to evaporate the ketone first, leaving a mixture of methanol and water. Then, use fractional distillation to evaporate the methanol. The resulting product contains very few impurities.

In summary, the main product is methanol, and the by-products include tar, coke, fuel gas, acetic acid, ketone, etc., all of which have wide applications in daily life and industry.

(2) The Method of Manufacturing Ethanol: The raw materials for making ethanol are generally sweet potatoes, corn flour, lactose, and other various starches and sugars, depending on the prices in different locations.

If the raw material is sugar, only two steps are required: fermentation and distillation. If the raw material is starch, it must first be converted into sugar and then fermented.

First, cook the starch with water for one hour to make a thin starch solution, and then mix it with malt (a type of fermenting agent, English name Malt) until the starch is converted into maltose at the appropriate time. Rinse it out with water to await the second step.

Dilute the sugar with water to make a 10% solution, and add 10% nutrient solution. This solution is synthesized from one gram each of potassium nitrate, magnesium chloride, calcium nitrate, and potassium phosphate, and one hundred cubic centimeters of water, to serve as food for the yeast! Then add a small amount of sulfuric acid to make the solution weakly acidic, so that other harmful bacteria cannot survive. Finally, mix in the yeast. During the fermentation period, a large amount of heat is released, so it must be properly monitored to ensure that the temperature does not exceed 100 degrees Fahrenheit. After about a week, distill this solution, and then redistill it (Rectirication), which yields 95% ethanol, containing very few impurities.

If the raw material is sugar, the fermentation and distillation procedures are the same.

The above is a long explanation, only giving a very simple description. If Mr. Pingzhang or other comrades want to research further, they can refer to various industrial chemistry books. Space is limited here, so I cannot describe everything in detail.

Rebirth Road

The Woes of a Shop Assistant 209

— Cangping

After much effort, I finally broke through after three years of sweeping floors and wiping tables, and became a shop assistant.

In my student days, looking forward to being a shop assistant was like a student looking forward to becoming a Ph.D. I thought that becoming a shop assistant would bring more wealth and that I could do more high-level things. I thought that the plans I had in mind could be realized, and I could gradually move up, from shop assistant to manager, from manager to boss. I thought that becoming a boss would bring wealth, and that with wealth, I could establish a business. I thought that everything in my ideal could be solved.

But in reality, it is not that easy. I started as a shop assistant at the age of seventeen, and now at the age of twenty-five, I am still a shop assistant. The experience and conditions I have gained from being a shop assistant for these nine years are as follows:

You should respect your superiors' orders. You cannot complain about the smell of their farts. You must be loyal to the boss and deceitful to others. You should shed every drop of sweat for him. Don't ask about the tens of thousands of gold coins he earns. If you are already married, it is best to have your wife live like a widow, while he has three or four concubines, and cannot be without them for a day. This is an entitlement he earned in his previous life. Most importantly, you cannot get too old. If you are full of sorrow and your eyes are dim, you should be sensible and roll up your bedding and go home, sparing him the trouble of saying it.

What chills me the most is that a shop assistant should not get sick. If an illness drags on, your job is at risk, and your salary will be stopped. Alas! I worry for the shop assistants who have no savings. I cry out loud for the shop assistants who are suffering from the same illness as me. Finally, I pray to God not to add to the suffering of the shop assistants. I silently wish that the old bosses would ease up on the whipping of us suffering and helpless shop assistants.

The Grand Exhibition of Xiong and Wang's Joint Works: The two gentlemen, Wang Zhongshan and Xiong Songquan, prominent painters, have been active in Shanghai for over thirty years. Their works are transcendent and refined, and have long been highly regarded in artistic circles. Recently, at the invitation of Mr. Xie Mengli of Lili Company, they are publicly exhibiting one hundred exquisite paintings created jointly by the two artists for five days. Every day, five to six hundred people have visited. Many have also been eager to commission paintings. Today is the fourth day.

Ms. Wang Lengying Sells Calligraphy to Relieve Famine: Hai'ning, Zhejiang, has been affected by the war, and the silk industry has been suspended. The residents are struggling to make a living, and cries of sorrow fill the land. Congee is currently being distributed. Famine victims from seven or eight miles around are coming to eat, supporting the old and leading the young. The scene is particularly tragic. Wang Lengying and Qingying are from a prominent family in Hai'ning and are skilled in calligraphy and painting. Thinking of the suffering of the elders and children in their hometown, they plan to donate all the proceeds from their calligraphy and painting. Gentlemen of benevolence in this era, if you wish to form a bond of ink and help the poor, please send your works to the Shanghai Women's Middle School or the Shanghai Women's Calligraphy and Painting Society at No. 10, Jiashi Lane, Menghua Street, Ximen.

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center at No. 80 Hualong Road, Shanghai, will hold its eighth service talk at 8:00 a.m. today in the center's auditorium. Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Yang Xixian, and Lin Kanghou have been invited to speak on issues related to youth employment and self-cultivation. People from all walks of life who wish to attend the lectures are welcome to take a seat at their convenience.

Summer Fine Soap: The Pears' Glycerine Soap, and the Child Brand and Golden Box Brand soaps, managed by the British firm Lao Jin Jiang Foreign Firm, are made purely with scientific methods, extracting glycerine and adding fragrance. During this hot weather, using it for washing your face and bathing can remove prickly heat and moisturize the skin, making it a good companion for the summer.
